practica de uso de paquete dplyr

Autor/a

Franchesca Moraga

Introduccion

Este documento contiene algunos ejemplos de uso de las funciones del paquete dplyr de [Tidyverse] (https//www.tydyverse.org/)

#Carga de paquetes

library(tidyverse)
library(palmerpenguins)
library(knitr)

Carga de datos

#|label: carga-datos
#| message : false
#| warning: false

delitos_2023 <- read_csv("estadisticaspoliciales2023.csv", locale = locale(encoding = "WINDOWS-1252"))
Rows: 49609 Columns: 12
── Column specification ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Delimiter: ","
chr (12): Delito, SubDelito, Fecha, Hora, Victima, SubVictima, Edad, Genero,...

ℹ Use `spec()` to retrieve the full column specification for this data.
ℹ Specify the column types or set `show_col_types = FALSE` to quiet this message.

select

Ejemplos 1

# select(penguins, spacies, bill_lengh_mm, sex)

penguins |>
  select(species, bill_length_mm, sex) |>
  head(10) |>
  kable()
species bill_length_mm sex
Adelie 39.1 male
Adelie 39.5 female
Adelie 40.3 female
Adelie NA NA
Adelie 36.7 female
Adelie 39.3 male
Adelie 38.9 female
Adelie 39.2 male
Adelie 34.1 NA
Adelie 42.0 NA

Ejemplos 2

penguins |>
  select(
    especie = species,
    logitud_pico_mm = bill_length_mm, sex) |> 
  head(10) |>
  kable()
especie logitud_pico_mm sex
Adelie 39.1 male
Adelie 39.5 female
Adelie 40.3 female
Adelie NA NA
Adelie 36.7 female
Adelie 39.3 male
Adelie 38.9 female
Adelie 39.2 male
Adelie 34.1 NA
Adelie 42.0 NA

filter()

Ejemplo 1

penguins |>
  select( species, island, sex) |>
  filter(species == "Adelie") |>
  filter(sex == "male") |> 
  filter(island == "Torgersen") |>
  kable()
species island sex
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male
Adelie Torgersen male

Ejemplon 2

# Delitos cometidos a vehiculos en el cantón de Montes de Oca 
delitos_2023 |>
  select(Delito, SubDelito, Victima, SubVictima, Canton, Distrito) |>
  filter(Canton == "MONTES DE OCA" & Victima == "VEHICULO" ) |>
  kable()

arrange()

Ejemplo 1

penguins |> 
  select(species, bill_length_mm, bill_depth_mm)|>
  head(12) |>
    arrange(bill_length_mm, bill_depth_mm)|>
  kable()
species bill_length_mm bill_depth_mm
Adelie 34.1 18.1
Adelie 36.7 19.3
Adelie 37.8 17.1
Adelie 37.8 17.3
Adelie 38.9 17.8
Adelie 39.1 18.7
Adelie 39.2 19.6
Adelie 39.3 20.6
Adelie 39.5 17.4
Adelie 40.3 18.0
Adelie 42.0 20.2
Adelie NA NA

mutate ()

penguins |> 
  select(species,sex, body_mass_g)|>
  mutate(body_mass_kg = body_mass_g/1000)|>
    mutate(body_mass_lb = body_mass_kg*2.2)|>
  head(12) |>
  kable()
species sex body_mass_g body_mass_kg body_mass_lb

Adelie female 3250 3.250 7.150

Ejemplo 2

delitos_2023 |>
  select(Delito, SubDelito,Fecha, Hora, Canton) |>
  mutate(Fecha_Date = as.Date(delitos_2023$Fecha, format="%d/%m/%Y"))|>
  filter(Canton == "MONTES DE OCA") |>
  arrange(Fecha_Date)|>
  kable()
Delito SubDelito Fecha Hora Canton Fecha_Date

# label: summarize-01

# Peso promedio por especie de pinguinos

penguins |> 
  group_by(species) |>
  summarize(
    body_mass_g_mean = mean(body_mass_g,na.rm = TRUE),
    body_mass_g_min = min(body_mass_g, na.rm = TRUE),
     body_mass_g_mAX = max(body_mass_g, na.rm = TRUE),
    cantidad_pinguinos = n()
    ) |>
  kable()
species body_mass_g_mean body_mass_g_min body_mass_g_mAX cantidad_pinguinos
Adelie 3700.662 2850 4775 152
Chinstrap 3733.088 2700 4800 68
Gentoo 5076.016 3950 6300 124 
aggregate(
  body_mass_g ~ species,
  data = penguins, 
  FUN = mean
  
)

# Cantidad d ehomicidios por provincia y canton
delitos_2023 |>
  filter(Delito == "HOMICIDIO") |>
  group_by(Provincia, Canton, Distrito, Genero) |>
   summarize(homicidios_2023 = n()
             )|>
  arrange(desc(homicidios_2023)) |>
      kable()
